
---NAYIBE JARAMILLO
/*2. Create 2 Tablespaces (0.125) :
a. first one with 2 Gb and 1 datafile, tablespace should be named " avianca " */

CREATE TABLESPACE AVIANCA DATAFILE 
'avianca1.dbf' SIZE 100M
AUTOEXTEND ON NEXT 1000K MAXSIZE 2048M
EXTENT MANAGEMENT LOCAL 
SEGMENT SPACE MANAGEMENT AUTO
ONLINE;

/*b. Undo tablespace with 25Mb of space and 1 datafile*/

CREATE UNDO TABLESPACE UNDO_TBS datafile
'UNDO_TBS1.dbf' size 25M
AUTOEXTEND OFF;
/*3. Set the undo tablespace to be used in the system (0.125)*/

ALTER SYSTEM SET UNDO_TABLESPACE = UNDO_TBS scope = both;

/*4. Create a DBA user (with the role DBA) and assign it to the tablespace called " avianca ", this user has
unlimited space on the tablespace (The user should have permission to connect) (0.125)*/

CREATE USER DBAUSER1 IDENTIFIED BY DBAUSER1
DEFAULT TABLESPACE  avianca
TEMPORARY TABLESPACE TEMP
QUOTA UNLIMITED ON avianca;

GRANT DBA TO DBAUSER1;
GRANT CONNECT, RESOURCE TO DBAUSER1;

/*5. Create 2 profiles. (0.125)
a. Profile 1: "clerk" password life 40 days, one session per user, 10 minutes idle, 4 failed login
attempts*/

CREATE PROFILE CLERKPROFILE LIMIT
SESSIONS_PER_USER 1
CPU_PER_SESSION UNLIMITED
CPU_PER_CALL UNLIMITED
CONNECT_TIME 240
IDLE_TIME 10
PRIVATE_SGA 20 M
FAILED_LOGIN_ATTEMPTS 4
PASSWORD_LIFE_TIME 40
PASSWORD_REUSE_MAX 4
PASSWORD_LOCK_TIME 1
PASSWORD_GRACE_TIME 2;
 

/*b. Profile 3: "development " password life 100 days, two session per user, 30 minutes idle, no
failed login attempts*/

CREATE PROFILE DEVELOPMENTPROFILE LIMIT 
SESSIONS_PER_USER 2
CPU_PER_SESSION UNLIMITED
CPU_PER_CALL UNLIMITED
CONNECT_TIME 240
IDLE_TIME 30
PRIVATE_SGA 20 M
--NO FAILED_LOGIN_ATTEMPTS 
PASSWORD_LIFE_TIME 100
PASSWORD_REUSE_MAX 5
PASSWORD_LOCK_TIME 1
PASSWORD_GRACE_TIME 2;

/*6. Create 4 users, assign them the tablespace " avianca "; 2 of them should have the clerk profile and the
remaining the development profile, all the users should be allow to connect to the database. (0.125)*/


CREATE USER USER1 IDENTIFIED BY USER1
DEFAULT TABLESPACE  AVIANCA
PROFILE CLERKPROFILE;

GRANT CREATE SESSION TO USER1;


CREATE USER USER2 IDENTIFIED BY USER2
DEFAULT TABLESPACE  AVIANCA
PROFILE CLERKPROFILE;

GRANT CREATE SESSION TO USER2;


CREATE USER USER3 IDENTIFIED BY USER3
DEFAULT TABLESPACE  AVIANCA
PROFILE DEVELOPMENTPROFILE;

GRANT CREATE SESSION TO USER3;

CREATE USER USER4 IDENTIFIED BY USER4
DEFAULT TABLESPACE  AVIANCA
PROFILE DEVELOPMENTPROFILE;

GRANT CREATE SESSION TO USER4;

/*7. Lock one user associate with clerk profile (0.125)*/

ALTER USER USER1 
ACCOUNT LOCK ;  





---------SIMON RESTREPO
/* 8. Create tables with its columns according to your normalization (0.125) */

CREATE TABLE empleados(
id int primary key,
tipo_empleado varchar(30),
nombre varchar(150),
apellido varchar(150),
sexo varchar(1),
fecha_nacimiento date,
antiguedad int,
fecha_ultimo_entrenamiento date,
direccion varchar(100),
email varchar(150),
celular varchar(20),
horas_descanso int,
estado varchar(30),
ubicacion_id int not null
);

CREATE TABLE pilotos(
id int primary key,
horas_vuelo int,
certificado_ICAO varchar(10),
tipo_cargo varchar(30),
empleado_id int,
licencia_id int
);


CREATE TABLE licencias(
id int primary key,
ATPL number (1),
CPL_IFR number (1),
CPL_ME number (1)
);

CREATE TABLE ciudades(
id int primary key,
ciudad varchar(30),
pais varchar(30)
);

CREATE TABLE itinerarios(
id int primary key,
pais_id int,
vuelo_id int,
aeropuerto_id int,
avion_id int,
fecha_real_salida timestamp,
fecha_real_llegada timestamp
);


CREATE TABLE itinerarios_x_check_in(
id int primary key,
itinerario_id int not null,
check_in_id int not null,
);

CREATE TABLE aeropuertos(
id int primary key,
nombre  varchar(200),
abreviatura varchar(20),
latitud number(18,5),
longitud number(18,5)
);


CREATE TABLE rutas(
id int primary key,
aeropuerto_origen_id int,
aeropuerto_destino_id int,
distancia_km int,
frecuencia_semanal int,
duracion_promedio int
);

CREATE TABLE vuelos(
id int primary key,
codigo_vuelo varchar(20),
ruta_id int not null,
tripulante_id int null
);



CREATE TABLE tripulantes(
id int primary key,
empleado_id int
);


CREATE TABLE check_in(
id int primary key,
pasajero_id int,
hora_check_in date,
nombre_contacto varchar(50),
telefono_contacto varchar(20),
email_contacto varchar(30),
pais_contacto varchar(30),
fecha_est_salida date,
fecha_est_llegada date
);

CREATE TABLE pasajeros(
id int primary key,
nombre varchar(50),
apellido varchar(50),
identificacion int,
tipo_documento int
);

CREATE TABLE aviones(
id  int primary key,
matricula varchar(30),
serial varchar(50),
edad int,
asientos_ejecutivos int,
asientos_economicos int,
asientos_estandar int
);

CREATE TABLE log_vuelos(
id int primary key,
time_stamp varchar(30),
hora_utc timestamp,
latitud varchar(20),
longitud varchar(20),
altitud varchar(20),
velocidad varchar(20),
direccion varchar(50)
);

/*foreign keys*/
                                          
ALTER TABLE empleados
add foreign key (ubicacion_id)
references ciudades(id);

ALTER TABLE pilotos
add foreign key (empleado_id)
references empleados(id);

ALTER TABLE pilotos
add foreign key (licencia_id)
references licencias(id);    

ALTER TABLE rutas
add foreign key (aeropuerto_origen_id)
references aeropuertos (id);

ALTER TABLE rutas
add foreign key (aeropuerto_destino_id)
references aeropuertos (id);

ALTER TABLE tripulantes
add foreign key (empleado_id)
references empleados (id);

ALTER TABLE vuelos
add foreign key (tripulante_id)
references tripulantes (id);  

ALTER TABLE vuelos
add foreign key (ruta_id)
references rutas (id);  

ALTER TABLE itinerarios
add foreign key (pais_id)
references ciudades (id);

ALTER TABLE itinerarios
add foreign key (aeropuerto_id)
references aeropuertos (id);

ALTER TABLE itinerarios
add foreign key (vuelo_id)
references vuelos (id);
  
ALTER TABLE itinerarios
add foreign key (avion_id)
references aviones (id);

ALTER TABLE itinerarios_x_check_in
add foreign key (check_in_id)
references check_in (id);

ALTER TABLE itinerarios_x_check_in
add foreign key (itinerario_id)
references intinerarios (id);

                                
/*CHECKS*/                                                     
ALTER TABLE empleados
ADD  CONSTRAINT  ck_tipo_empleado check (tipo_empleado in('PILOTO','Tripulante','Auxiliar de Servicio'));


ALTER TABLE empleados
ADD  CONSTRAINT  ck_estado_emp check (estado in('EN VUELO', 'ACTIVO', 'INACTIVO', 'JUBILADO', 'SUSPENDIDO', 'DESPEDIDO',
'ENTRENAMIENTO', 'LICENCIA', 'VACACIONES'));

ALTER TABLE pilotos
ADD  CONSTRAINT  ck_tipo_cargo check (tipo_cargo in('PILOTO','COPILOTO'));

ALTER TABLE pilotos
ADD  CONSTRAINT  ck_certificado_ICAO check (certificado_ICAO in('Nivel 1','Nivel 2','Nivel 3','Nivel 4','Nivel 5','Nivel 6'));

ALTER TABLE pasajeros
ADD  CONSTRAINT  ck_tipo_documento check (tipo_documento in('Cedula','Pasaporte','DNI','Cedula Extranjeria'));


ALTER TABLE rutas
ADD  CONSTRAINT  ck_frecuencia check (frecuencia_semanal in(8,2)); 


/*Create sequences for every primary key*/

create sequence id_empleado
increment by 1 
start with 1 minvalue 1; 

create sequence id_piloto
increment by 1 
start with 1 minvalue 1; 

create sequence id_ciudad
increment by 1 
start with 1 minvalue 1; 

create sequence id_licencia
increment by 1 
start with 1 minvalue 1; 

create sequence id_log_vuelo
increment by 1 
start with 1 minvalue 1; 


create sequence id_ruta
increment by 1 
start with 1 minvalue 1; 

create sequence id_itinerario
increment by 1 
start with 1 minvalue 1; 

create sequence id_avion
increment by 1 
start with 1 minvalue 1; 

create sequence id_tripulante
increment by 1 
start with 1 minvalue 1; 

create sequence id_vuelo
increment by 1 
start with 1 minvalue 1; 

create sequence id_aeropuerto
increment by 1 
start with 1 minvalue 1; 

create sequence id_check_in
increment by 1 
start with 1 minvalue 1; 

create sequence id_pasajero
increment by 1 
start with 1 minvalue 1;

create sequence id_itinerarios_x_check_in
increment by 1 
start with 1 minvalue 1;
